<div class="row how-it-works-content">
<div class="col-xs-12">
<h1>PS Deals - a unique PlayStation Games Price Tracker</h1>
<p><strong>PS Deals helps you track PlayStation games prices in the official PlayStation Store simply by subscribing to any game you'd like to buy. Let's see how it works:</strong></p>
<div class="row how-it-works-list">
<div class="how-it-works-list-item col-sm-4 col-xs-12">
<span class="list-number">1</span>
<span class="list-text">Choose your PlayStation console and region in the top menu</span>
</div>
<div class="how-it-works-list-item col-sm-4 col-xs-12">
<span class="list-number list-number-2">2</span>
<span class="list-text">Use search or go to the 'Explore' section to find any game you'd like to buy cheaper</span>
</div>
<div class="how-it-works-list-item col-sm-4 col-xs-12">
<span class="list-number list-number-3">3</span>
<span class="list-text">Press the 'Notify when price drops' button on the game page to receive free notification when the deal comes up</span>
</div>
</div>
<p>That's it! Now sit back and relax - we will notify you by email when the game's price in the official PlayStation Store drops. Also check all currently available deals in 'Discounts' section and don't forget to download <a href="https://apps.apple.com/app/ps-deals/id1076314983" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">PS Deals iOS app</a></p>
</div>
